A cancer cell line, called DLD1, is extremely sensitive to gene PRPS2 depletion via CRISPR-KO. Top 10 major dependencies for this cell line are: PRPS2, DUS2, NSUN2, SEC23A, NUDCD1, THUMPD1, SEC23B, DIAPH1, SATB2, HTRA2.
